c     *                                                                          *
c     *                                                                          *
c     * (1)   Modeling information and the detailed MCNP Model will only be      *
c     *       used for calculating and studying the results for validation       *
c     *       of neutronics computer codes and improvement of basic nuclear      *
c     *       cross section data.                                                *
c     *                                                                          *
c     * (2)   The model will not be used for any studies other than those        *
c     *       mentioned above.                                                   *
c     *                                                                          *
c     * (3)   Users of the "International Handbook of Evaluated Criticality      *
c     *       Safety Benchmark Experiments" will not distribute the model to     *

c     NW FLUX TRAP - ALUMINUM FILLER + PRESSURE TUBE + INSULATION TUBE
c     NE FLUX TRAP - NINE CO TARGETS IN 23 TARGET ARRAY
c      C FLUX TRAP - ONE  CO TARGET IN SEVEN POSITION ARRAY
c      E FLUX TRAP - SIX  CO TARGETS IN SEVEN TARGET ARRAY
c     SE FLUX TRAP - WATER IN FLOW TUBE + PRESSURE TUBE + INSULATION TUBE

c     SW FLUX TRAP - WATER IN FLOW TUBE + PRESSURE TUBE + INSULATION TUBE

c
